AN_check_culture_minorities = {
	hidden_effect = {
		#Export
		export_to_variable = {
			variable_name = AN_province_culture
			value = culture
		}
		# Remove Incorrect Minorities
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 0 } 
					is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture which = AN_province_culture }
					is_variable_equal = { which = AN_minority_culture value = 0 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 0 }
			clr_province_flag = AN_int_min
			clr_province_flag = AN_protect_min
			clr_province_flag = AN_expel_min
			clr_province_flag = AN_enslave_min
			remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_1
			remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_2
			remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_3
			remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_minority_culture_1
			remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_minority_culture_2
			remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_minority_culture_3
			remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_1
			remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_2
			remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_3
			remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_minority_culture_1
			remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_minority_culture_2
			remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_minority_culture_3
			remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_minority_culture_1
			remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_minority_culture_2
			remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_minority_culture_3
			remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_minority_culture_1
			remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_minority_culture_2
			remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_minority_culture_3
			remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_minority_culture_1
			remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_minority_culture_2
			remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_minority_culture_3
			remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_minority_culture_1
			remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_minority_culture_2
			remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_minority_culture_3
			remove_province_modifier = AN_native_minority_culture_1
			remove_province_modifier = AN_native_minority_culture_2
			remove_province_modifier = AN_native_minority_culture_3

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 0 } }
				}
				set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture value = AN_secondary_culture }
				set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 }
				set_variable = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 0 }
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_province_flag
					AN_int_sec = { clr_province_flag = AN_int_sec set_province_flag = AN_int_min }
					AN_protect_sec = { clr_province_flag = AN_protect_sec set_province_flag = AN_protect_min  }
					AN_expel_sec = { clr_province_flag = AN_expel_sec set_province_flag = AN_expel_min }
					AN_enslave_sec = { clr_province_flag = AN_enslave_sec set_province_flag = AN_enslave_min  }
				}
				remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_secondary_culture
				remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_secondary_culture
				remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture
				remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
				remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture
				remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture
				remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_secondary_culture
				remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture
				remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_1
				remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_2
				remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_3

			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 0 }
				set_variable = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 0 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { OR = { is_city = yes is_colony = yes } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 0 } }
				}
				#Secondary
				if = {
					limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_secondary_culture which = AN_minority_culture } }

					clr_province_flag = AN_int_sec
					clr_province_flag = AN_protect_sec
					clr_province_flag = AN_expel_sec
					clr_province_flag = AN_enslave_sec

					remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_3


					set_variable = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 0 }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 3 } }
						change_culture = variable:AN_minority_culture
						set_variable = {
							which = AN_minority_culture
							which = AN_province_culture
						}

						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_province_flag
							AN_int_maj = { clr_province_flag = AN_int_maj set_province_flag = AN_int_min }
							AN_int_min = { clr_province_flag = AN_int_min set_province_flag = AN_int_maj }
							AN_protect_maj = { clr_province_flag = AN_protect_maj set_province_flag = AN_protect_min }
							AN_protect_min = { clr_province_flag = AN_protect_min set_province_flag = AN_protect_maj }
							AN_expel_maj = { clr_province_flag = AN_expel_maj set_province_flag = AN_expel_min }
							AN_expel_min = { clr_province_flag = AN_expel_min set_province_flag = AN_expel_maj }
							AN_enslave_maj = { clr_province_flag = AN_enslave_maj set_province_flag = AN_enslave_min }
							AN_enslave_min = { clr_province_flag = AN_enslave_min set_province_flag = AN_enslave_maj }
						}
					}
					else = {
						change_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = AN_secondary_culture which = AN_province_culture } }

					clr_province_flag = AN_int_sec
					clr_province_flag = AN_protect_sec
					clr_province_flag = AN_expel_sec
					clr_province_flag = AN_enslave_sec

					remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_3


					set_variable = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 0 }
					subtract_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 }
				}
				#####

				if = {
					limit = { owner = { primary_culture = variable:PREV:AN_secondary_culture } }
					remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_3

					add_province_modifier = {
						name = AN_primary_secondary_culture
						duration = -1 hidden = yes
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { owner = { accepted_culture = variable:PREV:AN_secondary_culture culture_group = variable:PREV:AN_secondary_culture } }
					remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_3

					add_province_modifier = {
						name = AN_unified_secondary_culture
						duration = -1 hidden = yes
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { owner = { accepted_culture = variable:PREV:AN_secondary_culture } }
					clr_province_flag = AN_expel_sec
					clr_province_flag = AN_enslave_sec
					
					remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_3
					
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = AN_accepted_secondary_culture
						duration = -1 hidden = yes
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { culture_group = variable:PREV:AN_secondary_culture }
					remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_3
					
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
						duration = -1 hidden = yes
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { culture_group = variable:PREV:AN_secondary_culture } }
					if = {
						limit = { has_province_flag = AN_protect_sec }
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_3
						
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = AN_protected_secondary_culture
							duration = -1 hidden = yes
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_province_flag = AN_expel_sec }
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_3

						add_province_modifier = {
							name = AN_expelled_secondary_culture
							duration = -1 hidden = yes
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_province_flag = AN_enslave_sec }
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_3

						add_province_modifier = {
							name = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture
							duration = -1 hidden = yes
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { NOT = { OR = { has_province_flag = AN_protect_sec has_province_flag = AN_expel_sec has_province_flag = AN_enslave_sec } } }
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_secondary_culture_3

						add_province_modifier = {
							name = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture
							duration = -1 hidden = yes
						}
					}
				}
				#Majorities
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = { primary_culture = variable:PREV:AN_province_culture }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 3 } }
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_4
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = AN_primary_majority_culture_0
							duration = -1 hidden = yes
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 2 } }
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_4
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = AN_primary_majority_culture_1
							duration = -1 hidden = yes
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 } }
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_2
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_3
						remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_4
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_0
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_1
						remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_2

					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_minority_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_minority_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_minority_culture_3
					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_0
					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_3
					remove_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_4
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_minority_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_minority_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_minority_culture_3
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_0
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_3
					remove_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_4
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_minority_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_minority_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_minority_culture_3
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_0
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_3
					remove_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_4
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_minority_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_minority_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_minority_culture_3
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_0
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_3
					remove_province_modifier = AN_expelled_majority_culture_4
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_minority_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_minority_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_minority_culture_3
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_0
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_3
					remove_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_4
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_minority_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_minority_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_minority_culture_3
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_0
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_1
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_2
					remove_province_modifier = AN_native_majority_culture_3

					add_province_modifier = {
						name = AN_native_majority_culture_4
						duration = -1 #hidden = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### SET TARGET

AN_check_culture_process = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_overseas = yes
				island = yes
				AND = { #C Maj, NC Min
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_minority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_minority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_minority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_minority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_minority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_minority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_minority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_minority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_minority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_minority_culture_3
					}
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_3
					}
					NOT = { OR = { has_province_flag = AN_int_maj has_province_flag = AN_expel_min } }
				}
				AND = { #C Maj, NC Sec
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture_3
					}
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_majority_culture_3
					}
					NOT = { OR = { has_province_flag = AN_int_maj has_province_flag = AN_expel_sec } }
				}
				AND = { #NC Maj, C Min
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_minority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_minority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_minority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_minority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_minority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_minority_culture_3
					}
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_3
					}
					NOT = { OR = { has_province_flag = AN_int_min has_province_flag = AN_expel_maj } }
				}
				AND = { #NC Maj, C Sec
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_secondary_culture
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_secondary_culture
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
					}
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_3
					}
					NOT = { OR = { has_province_flag = AN_int_sec has_province_flag = AN_expel_maj } }
				}
				AND = { #NC Min, C Sec
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_secondary_culture
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_secondary_culture
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_secondary_culture
					}
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_majority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_majority_culture_3
					}
					NOT = { OR = { has_province_flag = AN_int_sec has_province_flag = AN_expel_min } }
				}
				AND = { #C Min, NC Sec
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_primary_minority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_minority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_minority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_unified_minority_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_minority_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_minority_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_coexisting_minority_culture_3
					}
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_protected_secondary_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_accepted_secondary_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_non_accepted_secondary_culture_3
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture_1
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture_2
						has_province_modifier = AN_enslaved_secondary_culture_3
					}
					NOT = { OR = { has_province_flag = AN_int_min has_province_flag = AN_expel_sec } }
				}
			}
		}
		AN_select_target_culture = yes
	}
}

AN_set_target_culture = {
	16000 = {
		change_culture = $CULTURE$
		export_to_variable = {
			variable_name = AN_target_culture
			value = culture
		}
		PREV = { set_variable = { which = AN_target_culture which = PREV } }
	}
}

AN_select_target_culture = {

	##### FRENCH CHECKS #####
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { culture_group = french }
			OR = {
				culture_group = french
				minority_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=french }
				secondary_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=french }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = norman
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=norman }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=norman }
					province_group = normandy_group
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=normand }
		}
		else_if = { ###edit
			limit = {
				#OR = {
					#culture =
					#minority_culture = { CULTURE= }
					#secondary_culture = { CULTURE= }
					colonial_region = colonial_acadia
				#}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=moselle }
		}
		else_if = { ###edit
			limit = {
				#OR = {
					#culture =
					#minority_culture = { CULTURE= }
					#secondary_culture = { CULTURE= }
					colonial_region = colonial_acadia
				#}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=rhenan }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture_group = arpitan_g
					minority_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=arpitan_g }
					secondary_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=arpitan_g }
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=arpitan }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture_group = occitan
					minority_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=occitan }
					secondary_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=occitan }
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=meridionale }
		}
		else_if = { ###edit
			limit = {
				#OR = {
					#culture =
					#minority_culture = { CULTURE= }
					#secondary_culture = { CULTURE= }
					colonial_region = colonial_acadia
				#}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=alpin }
		}
		else_if = { ###edit
			limit = {
				#OR = {
					#culture =
					#minority_culture = { CULTURE= }
					#secondary_culture = { CULTURE= }
					colonial_region = colonial_acadia
				#}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=alpin }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = corsican_culture
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=corsican_culture }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=corsican_culture }
					culture = corsa
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=corsa }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=corsa }
					area = corsica_sardinia_area
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=corse }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = sardinian
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=sardinian }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=sardinian }
					culture = sarda
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=sarda }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=sarda }
					culture = sardynya

					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=sardynya }
					province_group = sardinia_group
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=sarde }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = sicilian
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=sicilian }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=sicilian }
					culture = siceliot
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=siceliot }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=siceliot }
					culture_group = siculu
					minority_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=siculu }
					secondary_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=siculu }
					culture = siciliana
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=siciliana }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=siciliana }
					culture = siqilliya
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=siqilliya }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=siqilliya }
					province_group = sicily_group
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=sicilienne }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = levantini
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=levantini }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=levantini }

					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=poulain }

				region = mashriq_region
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=frankolevantin }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				#OR = {
					#culture =

				#}

			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=acadien }
		}

				}
			}

		}

				OR = {
					culture = finnish

					culture = west_karelian

					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=west_karelian }

		}

					culture = estonian
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=estonian }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=estonian }
					culture = voro
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=voro }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=voro }
					area = estonia_ingria_area
					area = north_livonia_area
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=estlandic }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = livonian
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=livonian }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=livonian }
					culture_group = baltic
					minority_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=baltic }
					secondary_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=baltic }
					area = livonia_area

					area = latgallia_area
					area = semigallia_area
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=livlandic }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					#culture =
					#minority_culture = { CULTURE= }
					#secondary_culture = { CULTURE= }
					area = greenland_area
					area = east_greenland_area
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=gronlandsk }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {

		else_if = {

				OR = {
					#culture =
					#minority_culture_group = { CULTURE= }
					#secondary_culture_group = { CULTURE= }
					region = hudson_bay_region
				}
			}

	}
	####################

	##### IRANIAN CHECKS #####
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { culture_group = iranian }
			OR = {
				culture_group = iranian
				minority_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=iranian }
				secondary_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=iranian }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = khuzestani
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=khuzestani }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=khuzestani }
					area = khuzestan_area
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=khuzi }
		}
	}
	####################

	##### SAKA CHECKS #####
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { culture_group = east_iranian }
			OR = {
				culture_group = east_iranian
				minority_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=east_iranian }
				secondary_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=east_iranian }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = horasanli
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=horasanli }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=horasanli }
					culture = khorasani
					minority_culture = { CULTURE=khorasani }
					secondary_culture = { CULTURE=khorasani }
					region = khorasan_region
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=xorasani }
		}
	}
	####################

	##### JEWISH CHECKS #####
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { culture_group = jewish_culture_group }
			OR = {
				culture_group = jewish_culture_group
				minority_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=jewish_culture_group }
				secondary_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=jewish_culture_group }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				continent = asia
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						region = caucasia_region
						superregion = siberia_superregion
					}
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=mizrahi }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				region = iberia_region
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=sephardi }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					superregion = europe_superregion
					region = north_german_region
					region = south_german_region
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=ashkenazi }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture_group = latin
					minority_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=latin }
					secondary_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=latin }
					region = italy_region
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=italkim }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture_group = byzantine_g
					minority_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=byzantine_g }
					secondary_culture_group = { CULTURE_GROUP=byzantine_g }
					region = balkan_region
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=rhomaniot }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					region = poland_region
					superregion = eastern_europe_superregion
				}
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=knaanic }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				region = caucasia_region
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=juhuro }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				region = horn_of_africa_superregion
			}
			AN_set_target_culture = { CULTURE=beta_israeli }
		}
	}
	####################
}
### MINORITY INTERACTIONS

change_minority_culture = {
	#custom_tooltip = AN_$CULTURE$_$SIZE$_minority.tooltip
	hidden_effect = {
		16000 = {
			change_culture = $CULTURE$
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = AN_minority_culture
				value = culture
			}
			PREV = {
				set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture which = PREV }
				#set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = $SIZE$ }
			}
		}
	}
	AN_check_culture_minorities = yes
}

change_secondary_culture = {
	#custom_tooltip = AN_$CULTURE$_secondary.tooltip
	hidden_effect = {
		16000 = {
			change_culture = $CULTURE$
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = AN_secondary_culture
				value = culture
			}
			PREV = {
				set_variable = { which = AN_secondary_culture which = PREV }
			}
		}
	}
	AN_check_culture_minorities = yes
}

AN_set_minority_culture = {
	custom_tooltip = AN_$CULTURE$_$SIZE$_minority.tooltip
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 } }
		custom_tooltip = AN_set_minority_culture_replace.tooltip
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		16000 = {
			change_culture = $CULTURE$
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = AN_minority_culture
				value = culture
			}
			PREV = {
				set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture which = PREV }
				set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = $SIZE$ }
			}
		}
	}
	AN_check_culture_minorities = yes
}

AN_set_secondary_culture = {
	custom_tooltip = AN_$CULTURE$_sec_culture.tooltip
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 1 } }
		custom_tooltip = AN_set_secondary_culture_replace.tooltip
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		16000 = {
			change_culture = $CULTURE$
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = AN_secondary_culture
				value = culture
			}
			PREV = {
				set_variable = { which = AN_secondary_culture which = PREV }
			}
		}
	}
	AN_check_culture_minorities = yes
}

AN_increase_culture_size = {
	if = {
		limit = { culture = $CULTURE$ }
		custom_tooltip = AN_increase_$CULTURE$_maj_culture.tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 } }
			hidden_effect = { 
				subtract_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_base_manpower = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { minority_culture = { CULTURE=$CULTURE$ } }
		custom_tooltip = AN_increase_$CULTURE$_min_culture.tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 4 } }
				change_culture = variable:PREV:AN_minority_culture
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = {
						which = AN_minority_culture
						which = AN_province_culture
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_province_flag
						AN_int_maj = { clr_province_flag = AN_int_maj set_province_flag = AN_int_min }
						AN_int_min = { clr_province_flag = AN_int_min set_province_flag = AN_int_maj }
						AN_protect_maj = { clr_province_flag = AN_protect_maj set_province_flag = AN_protect_min }
						AN_protect_min = { clr_province_flag = AN_protect_min set_province_flag = AN_protect_maj }
						AN_expel_maj = { clr_province_flag = AN_expel_maj set_province_flag = AN_expel_min }
						AN_expel_min = { clr_province_flag = AN_expel_min set_province_flag = AN_expel_maj }
						AN_enslave_maj = { clr_province_flag = AN_enslave_maj set_province_flag = AN_enslave_min }
						AN_enslave_min = { clr_province_flag = AN_enslave_min set_province_flag = AN_enslave_maj }
					}
					set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 3 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { secondary_culture = { CULTURE=$CULTURE$ } }
		custom_tooltip = AN_replace_$CULTURE$_min_culture.tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = AN_secondary_culture
				which = AN_minority_culture
			}
			16000 = {
				change_culture = $CULTURE$
				export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = AN_minority_culture
					value = culture
				}
				PREV = {
					set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture which = PREV }
				}
			}
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_province_flag
				AN_int_sec = { clr_province_flag = AN_int_sec set_province_flag = AN_int_min }
				AN_int_min = { clr_province_flag = AN_int_min set_province_flag = AN_int_sec }
				AN_protect_sec = { clr_province_flag = AN_protect_sec set_province_flag = AN_protect_min }
				AN_protect_min = { clr_province_flag = AN_protect_min set_province_flag = AN_protect_sec }
				AN_expel_sec = { clr_province_flag = AN_expel_sec set_province_flag = AN_expel_min }
				AN_expel_min = { clr_province_flag = AN_expel_min set_province_flag = AN_expel_sec }
				AN_enslave_sec = { clr_province_flag = AN_enslave_sec set_province_flag = AN_enslave_min }
				AN_enslave_min = { clr_province_flag = AN_enslave_min set_province_flag = AN_enslave_sec }
			}
			set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 2 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 } }
			custom_tooltip = AN_$CULTURE$_sec_culture.tooltip
			hidden_effect = {
				16000 = {
					change_culture = $CULTURE$
					export_to_variable = {
						variable_name = AN_secondary_culture
						value = culture
					}
					PREV = {
						set_variable = { which = AN_minority_secondary which = PREV }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = AN_$CULTURE$_1_minority.tooltip
			hidden_effect = {
				16000 = {
					change_culture = $CULTURE$
					export_to_variable = {
						variable_name = AN_minority_culture
						value = culture
					}
					PREV = {
						set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture which = PREV }
					}
				}
				set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 1 }
			}
		}
		
	}
	AN_check_culture_minorities = yes
}

AN_decrease_minority_culture_size = {
	custom_tooltip = AN_change_minority_culture_size_d.tooltip
	hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = -1 } }
	AN_check_culture_minorities = yes
}

AN_remove_minority_culture = {
	custom_tooltip = AN_remove_minority_culture.tooltip
	hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = AN_minority_culture_size value = 0 } }
	AN_check_culture_minorities = yes
}

AN_remove_secondary_culture = {
	custom_tooltip = AN_remove_secondary_culture.tooltip
	hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = AN_secondary_culture value = 0 } }
	AN_check_culture_minorities = yes
}
